    42	async function run() {

    44	
    45	  eprintln(header())
    46	  eprintln()
    47	
    48	  let cleanup: (() => void)[] = []

    50	  if (!flags['--force']) {

    53	      error('Git directory is not clean. Please stash or commit your changes before migrating.')

    55	        `You may use the ${highlight('--force')} flag to silence this warning and perform the migration.`,
    56	      )
    57	      process.exit(1)
    58	    }
    59	  }
    60	
    61	  {
    62	    // Stylesheet migrations
    63	
    64	    // Use provided files
    65	    let files = flags._.map((file) => path.resolve(base, file))
    66	
    67	    // Discover CSS files in case no files were provided
    68	    if (files.length === 0) {
    69	      info('Searching for CSS files in the current directory and its subdirectories…')
    70

    74	        // gitignore: true will first search for all .gitignore including node_modules folders, this makes the initial search much faster

    84

    86	    for (let result of loadResults) {
    87	      if (result.status === 'rejected') {
    88	        error(`${result.reason?.message ?? result.reason}`, { prefix: '↳ ' })
    89	      }
    90	    }
    91	
    92	    let stylesheets = loadResults
    93	      .filter((result) => result.status === 'fulfilled')
    94	      .map((result) => result.value)
    95	    let originals = new Map(stylesheets.map((sheet) => [sheet, sheet.root.toString()]))
    96	
    97	    // Analyze the stylesheets
    98	    try {
    99	      await analyzeStylesheets(stylesheets)
   100	    } catch (e: any) {
   101	      error(`${e?.message ?? e}`, { prefix: '↳ ' })
   102	    }
   103	
   104	    // Ensure stylesheets are linked to configs. But this is only necessary when
   105	    // migrating from v3 to v4.
   106	    if (version.isMajor(3)) {

   108	        await linkConfigsToStylesheets(stylesheets, {

   116

   126	    for (let sheet of stylesheets) {

   128	      if (!version.isMajor(3) && !sheet.linkedConfigPath) continue
   129	
   130	      let config = await prepareConfig(sheet.linkedConfigPath, { base })
   131	      configBySheet.set(sheet, config)

   138	      jsConfigMigrationBySheet.set(sheet, jsConfigMigration)
   139	
   140	      if (jsConfigMigration !== null) {

   142	        cleanup.push(() => fs.rm(config.configFilePath))
   143	      }

   145	      if (jsConfigMigration !== null) {

   149	        )
   150	      }

   152

   154	    if (stylesheets.length > 0) {

   166	                config ??= configBySheet.get(parent)!

   182	        }
   183	      }),

   185

   190	      } catch (e: any) {
   191	        error(`${e?.message ?? e}`, { prefix: '↳ ' })
   192	      }
   193	
   194	      // Cleanup `@import "…" layer(utilities)`
   195	      for (let sheet of stylesheets) {
   196	        for (let importRule of sheet.importRules) {
   197	          if (!importRule.raws.tailwind_injected_layer) continue

   200	          )
   201	          if (!importedSheet) continue
   202	
   203	          // Only remove the `layer(…)` next to the import if any of the children

   205	          if (

   209	          }

   211	          // Make sure to remove the `layer(…)` from the `@import` at-rule
   212	          importRule.params = importRule.params.replace(/ layer\([^)]+\)/, '').trim()

   216

   221	    }
   222	
   223	    // Write all files to disk

   226	
   227	      await fs.writeFile(sheet.file, sheet.root.toString())
   228	
   229	      if (sheet.isTailwindRoot) {
   230	        success(`Migrated stylesheet: ${highlight(relative(sheet.file, base))}`, { prefix: '↳ ' })
   231	      }
   232	    }
   233	
   234	    info('Updating dependencies…')
   235	    {
   236	      let pkgManager = pkg(base)
   237	      let dependencies = [
   238	        'tailwindcss',
   239	        '@tailwindcss/cli',
   240	        '@tailwindcss/postcss',
   241	        '@tailwindcss/vite',
   242	        '@tailwindcss/node',

   246	      try {

   248	        for (let dependency of dependencies) {

   250	        }
   251	      } catch {}

   253	
   254	    let tailwindRootStylesheets = stylesheets.filter((sheet) => sheet.isTailwindRoot && sheet.file)

   263	      // Template migrations
   264	      for (let sheet of tailwindRootStylesheets) {
   265	        let compiler = await sheet.compiler()
   266	        if (!compiler) continue
   267	        let designSystem = await sheet.designSystem()
   268	        if (!designSystem) continue
   269	
   270	        // Figure out the source files to migrate
   271	        let sources = (() => {
   272	          // Disable auto source detection
   273	          if (compiler.root === 'none') {
   274	            return []
   275	          }
   276	
   277	          // No root specified, use the base directory
   278	          if (compiler.root === null) {
   279	            return [{ base, pattern: '**/*', negated: false }]
   280	          }
   281	
   282	          // Use the specified root

   286	        let config = configBySheet.get(sheet)

   292	          seenFiles.add(file)
   293	          filesToMigrate.push(file)
   294	        }
   295	
   296	        // Migrate each file
   297	        await Promise.allSettled(
   298	          filesToMigrate.map((file) =>
   299	            migrateTemplate(designSystem, config?.userConfig ?? null, file),
   300	          ),
   301	        )
   302	
   303	        if (config?.configFilePath) {
   304	          success(
   305	            `Migrated templates for configuration file: ${highlight(relative(config.configFilePath, base))}`,
   306	            { prefix: '↳ ' },
   307	          )
   308	        } else {
   309	          success(
   310	            `Migrated templates for: ${highlight(relative(sheet.file ?? '<unknown>', base))}`,
   311	            {
   312	              prefix: '↳ ',
   313	            },
   314	          )
   315	        }
   316	      }
   317	    }
   318	  }
   319	
   320	  if (version.isMajor(3)) {
   321	    // PostCSS config migration
   322	    await migratePostCSSConfig(base)
   323	  }
   324	
   325	  // Run all cleanup functions because we completed the migration
   326	  await Promise.allSettled(cleanup.map((fn) => fn()))
   327	
   328	  // Figure out if we made any changes
   329	  if (isRepoDirty()) {
   330	    success('Verify the changes and commit them to your repository.')
   331	  } else {
   332	    success('No changes were made to your repository.')
   333	  }
   334	}

    32	  designSystem: DesignSystem,

    34	  rawCandidate: string,

    37	export const DEFAULT_MIGRATIONS: Migration[] = [
    38	  migrateEmptyArbitraryValues,
    39	  migratePrefix,
    40	  migrateCanonicalizeCandidate,
    41	  migrateBgGradient,
    42	  migrateSimpleLegacyClasses,

    59	
    60	let migrateCached = new DefaultMap<
    61	  DesignSystem,
    62	  DefaultMap<Config | null, DefaultMap<string, Promise<string>>>
    63	>((designSystem) => {
    64	  return new DefaultMap((userConfig) => {
    65	    return new DefaultMap(async (rawCandidate) => {
    66	      let original = rawCandidate
    67	
    68	      for (let migration of DEFAULT_MIGRATIONS) {
    69	        rawCandidate = await migration(designSystem, userConfig, rawCandidate)
    70	      }
    71	
    72	      // Verify that the candidate actually makes sense at all. E.g.: `duration`
    73	      // is not a valid candidate, but it will parse because `duration-<number>`
    74	      // exists.
    75	      let signature = computeUtilitySignature.get(designSystem).get(rawCandidate)
    76	      if (typeof signature !== 'string') return original
    77	
    78	      return rawCandidate
    79	    })
    80	  })
    81	})
    82	
    83	export async function migrateCandidate(
    84	  designSystem: DesignSystem,
    85	  userConfig: Config | null,
    86	  rawCandidate: string,
    87	  // Location is only set when migrating a candidate from a source file
    88	  location?: {
    89	    contents: string
    90	    start: number
    91	    end: number
    92	  },
    93	): Promise<string> {
    94	  // Skip this migration if we think that the migration is unsafe
    95	  if (location && !isSafeMigration(rawCandidate, location, designSystem)) {
    96	    return rawCandidate
    97	  }
    98	
    99	  return migrateCached.get(designSystem).get(userConfig).get(rawCandidate)
   100	}
   101	
   102	export default async function migrateContents(
   103	  designSystem: DesignSystem,
   104	  userConfig: Config | null,
   105	  contents: string,
   106	  extension: string,
   107	): Promise<string> {
   108	  let candidates = await extractRawCandidates(contents, extension)
   109	
   110	  let changes: StringChange[] = []
   111	
   112	  for (let { rawCandidate, start, end } of candidates) {
   113	    let migratedCandidate = await migrateCandidate(designSystem, userConfig, rawCandidate, {
   114	      contents,
   115	      start,
   116	      end,
   117	    })
   118	
   119	    if (migratedCandidate === rawCandidate) {
   120	      continue
   121	    }
   122	
   123	    changes.push({
   124	      start,
   125	      end,
   126	      replacement: migratedCandidate,
   127	    })
   128	  }
   129	
   130	  return spliceChangesIntoString(contents, changes)
   131	}
   132	
   133	export async function migrate(designSystem: DesignSystem, userConfig: Config | null, file: string) {
   134	  let fullPath = path.isAbsolute(file) ? file : path.resolve(process.cwd(), file)
   135	  let contents = await fs.readFile(fullPath, 'utf-8')
   136	
   137	  await fs.writeFile(
   138	    fullPath,
   139	    await migrateContents(designSystem, userConfig, contents, extname(file)),
   140	  )
   141	}

     1	import { Scanner } from '@tailwindcss/oxide'
     2	import type { Candidate } from '../../../../tailwindcss/src/candidate'
     3	import type { DesignSystem } from '../../../../tailwindcss/src/design-system'
     4	
     5	export async function extractRawCandidates(
     6	  content: string,
     7	  extension: string = 'html',
     8	): Promise<{ rawCandidate: string; start: number; end: number }[]> {
     9	  let scanner = new Scanner({})
    10	  let result = scanner.getCandidatesWithPositions({ content, extension })
    11	
    12	  let candidates: { rawCandidate: string; start: number; end: number }[] = []
    13	  for (let { candidate: rawCandidate, position: start } of result) {
    14	    candidates.push({ rawCandidate, start, end: start + rawCandidate.length })
    15	  }
    16	  return candidates
    17	}
    18	
    19	// Create a basic stripped candidate without variants or important flag
    20	export function baseCandidate<T extends Candidate>(candidate: T) {
    21	  let base = structuredClone(candidate)
    22	
    23	  base.important = false
    24	  base.variants = []
    25	
    26	  return base
    27	}
    28	
    29	export function parseCandidate(designSystem: DesignSystem, input: string) {
    30	  return designSystem.parseCandidate(
    31	    designSystem.theme.prefix && !input.startsWith(`${designSystem.theme.prefix}:`)
    32	      ? `${designSystem.theme.prefix}:${input}`
    33	      : input,
    34	  )
    35	}
    36	
    37	export function printUnprefixedCandidate(designSystem: DesignSystem, candidate: Candidate) {
    38	  let candidateString = designSystem.printCandidate(candidate)
    39	
    40	  return designSystem.theme.prefix && candidateString.startsWith(`${designSystem.theme.prefix}:`)
    41	    ? candidateString.slice(designSystem.theme.prefix.length + 1)
    42	    : candidateString
    43	}

Here's the result of running `cat -n` on /testbed/packages/@tailwindcss-upgrade/src/codemods/template/is-safe-migration.ts:
     1	import { parseCandidate } from '../../../../tailwindcss/src/candidate'
     2	import type { DesignSystem } from '../../../../tailwindcss/src/design-system'
     3	import { DefaultMap } from '../../../../tailwindcss/src/utils/default-map'
     4	import * as version from '../../utils/version'
     5	
     6	const QUOTES = ['"', "'", '`']
     7	const LOGICAL_OPERATORS = ['&&', '||', '?', '===', '==', '!=', '!==', '>', '>=', '<', '<=']
     8	const CONDITIONAL_TEMPLATE_SYNTAX = [
     9	  // Vue
    10	  /v-else-if=['"]$/,
    11	  /v-if=['"]$/,
    12	  /v-show=['"]$/,
    13	  /(?<!:?class)=['"]$/,
    14	
    15	  // Alpine
    16	  /x-if=['"]$/,
    17	  /x-show=['"]$/,
    18	  /wire:[^\s]*?$/,
    19	]
    20	const NEXT_PLACEHOLDER_PROP = /placeholder=\{?['"]$/
    21	const VUE_3_EMIT = /\b\$?emit\(['"]$/
    22	
    23	export function isSafeMigration(
    24	  rawCandidate: string,
    25	  location: { contents: string; start: number; end: number },
    26	  designSystem: DesignSystem,
    27	): boolean {
    28	  // Ensure we are not migrating a candidate in a `<style>` block. The heuristic
    29	  // would be if the candidate is preceded by a whitespace and followed by a
    30	  // colon and whitespace.
    31	  //
    32	  // E.g.:
    33	  // ```vue
    34	  // <template>
    35	  //   <div class="foo"></div>
    36	  // </template>
    37	  //
    38	  //
    39	  // <style>
    40	  // .foo {
    41	  //   flex-shrink: 0;
    42	  //  ^           ^^
    43	  // }
    44	  // </style>
    45	  // ```
    46	  if (
    47	    // Whitespace before the candidate
    48	    location.contents[location.start - 1]?.match(/\s/) &&
    49	    // A colon followed by whitespace after the candidate
    50	    location.contents.slice(location.end, location.end + 2)?.match(/^:\s/)
    51	  ) {
    52	    // Compute all `<style>` ranges once and cache it for the current files
    53	    let ranges = styleBlockRanges.get(location.contents)
    54	
    55	    for (let i = 0; i < ranges.length; i += 2) {
    56	      let start = ranges[i]
    57	      let end = ranges[i + 1]
    58	
    59	      // Check if the candidate is inside a `<style>` block
    60	      if (location.start >= start && location.end <= end) {
    61	        return false
    62	      }
    63	    }
    64	  }
    65	
    66	  let [candidate] = parseCandidate(rawCandidate, designSystem)
    67	
    68	  // If we can't parse the candidate, then it's not a candidate at all. However,
    69	  // we could be dealing with legacy classes like `tw__flex` in Tailwind CSS v3
    70	  // land, which also wouldn't parse.
    71	  //
    72	  // So let's only skip if we couldn't parse and we are not in Tailwind CSS v3.
    73	  //
    74	  if (!candidate && version.isGreaterThan(3)) {
    75	    return false
    76	  }
    77	
    78	  // Parsed a candidate successfully, verify if it's a valid candidate
    79	  else if (candidate) {
    80	    // When we have variants, we can assume that the candidate is safe to migrate
    81	    // because that requires colons.
    82	    //
    83	    // E.g.: `hover:focus:flex`
    84	    if (candidate.variants.length > 0) {
    85	      return true
    86	    }
    87	
    88	    // When we have an arbitrary property, the candidate has such a particular
    89	    // structure it's very likely to be safe.
    90	    //
    91	    // E.g.: `[color:red]`
    92	    if (candidate.kind === 'arbitrary') {
    93	      return true
    94	    }
    95	
    96	    // A static candidate is very likely safe if it contains a dash.
    97	    //
    98	    // E.g.: `items-center`
    99	    if (candidate.kind === 'static' && candidate.root.includes('-')) {
   100	      return true
   101	    }
   102	
   103	    // A functional candidate is very likely safe if it contains a value (which
   104	    // implies a `-`). Or if the root contains a dash.
   105	    //
   106	    // E.g.: `bg-red-500`, `bg-position-20`
   107	    if (
   108	      (candidate.kind === 'functional' && candidate.value !== null) ||
   109	      (candidate.kind === 'functional' && candidate.root.includes('-'))
   110	    ) {
   111	      return true
   112	    }
   113	
   114	    // If the candidate contains a modifier, it's very likely to be safe because
   115	    // it implies that it contains a `/`.
   116	    //
   117	    // E.g.: `text-sm/7`
   118	    if (candidate.kind === 'functional' && candidate.modifier) {
   119	      return true
   120	    }
   121	  }
   122	
   123	  let currentLineBeforeCandidate = ''
   124	  for (let i = location.start - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
   125	    let char = location.contents.at(i)!
   126	    if (char === '\n') {
   127	      break
   128	    }
   129	    currentLineBeforeCandidate = char + currentLineBeforeCandidate
   130	  }
   131	  let currentLineAfterCandidate = ''
   132	  for (let i = location.end; i < location.contents.length; i++) {
   133	    let char = location.contents.at(i)!
   134	    if (char === '\n') {
   135	      break
   136	    }
   137	    currentLineAfterCandidate += char
   138	  }
   139	
   140	  // Heuristic: Require the candidate to be inside quotes
   141	  let isQuoteBeforeCandidate = QUOTES.some((quote) => currentLineBeforeCandidate.includes(quote))
   142	  let isQuoteAfterCandidate = QUOTES.some((quote) => currentLineAfterCandidate.includes(quote))
   143	  if (!isQuoteBeforeCandidate || !isQuoteAfterCandidate) {
   144	    return false
   145	  }
   146	
   147	  // Heuristic: Disallow object access immediately following the candidate
   148	  if (currentLineAfterCandidate[0] === '.') {
   149	    return false
   150	  }
   151	
   152	  // Heuristic: Disallow function call expressions immediately following the candidate
   153	  if (currentLineAfterCandidate.trim().startsWith('(')) {
   154	    return false
   155	  }
   156	
   157	  // Heuristic: Disallow logical operators preceding or following the candidate
   158	  for (let operator of LOGICAL_OPERATORS) {
   159	    if (
   160	      currentLineAfterCandidate.trim().startsWith(operator) ||
   161	      currentLineBeforeCandidate.trim().endsWith(operator)
   162	    ) {
   163	      return false
   164	    }
   165	  }
   166	
   167	  // Heuristic: Disallow conditional template syntax
   168	  for (let rule of CONDITIONAL_TEMPLATE_SYNTAX) {
   169	    if (rule.test(currentLineBeforeCandidate)) {
   170	      return false
   171	    }
   172	  }
   173	
   174	  // Heuristic: Disallow Next.js Image `placeholder` prop
   175	  if (NEXT_PLACEHOLDER_PROP.test(currentLineBeforeCandidate)) {
   176	    return false
   177	  }
   178	
   179	  // Heuristic: Disallow replacements inside `emit('…', …)`
   180	  if (VUE_3_EMIT.test(currentLineBeforeCandidate)) {
   181	    return false
   182	  }
   183	
   184	  return true
   185	}
   186	
   187	// Assumptions:
   188	// - All `<style` tags appear before the next `</style>` tag
   189	// - All `<style` tags are closed with `</style>`
   190	// - No nested `<style>` tags
   191	const styleBlockRanges = new DefaultMap((source: string) => {
   192	  let ranges: number[] = []
   193	  let offset = 0
   194	
   195	  while (true) {
   196	    let startTag = source.indexOf('<style', offset)
   197	    if (startTag === -1) return ranges
   198	
   199	    offset = startTag + 1
   200	
   201	    // Ensure the style looks like:
   202	    // - `<style>`   (closed)
   203	    // - `<style …>` (with attributes)
   204	    if (!source[startTag + 6].match(/[>\s]/)) continue
   205	
   206	    let endTag = source.indexOf('</style>', offset)
   207	    if (endTag === -1) return ranges
   208	    offset = endTag + 1
   209	
   210	    ranges.push(startTag, endTag)
   211	  }

    53	fn init_tracing() {
    54	    if !*SHOULD_TRACE {
    55	        return;
    56	    }
    57	
    58	    let file_path = format!("tailwindcss-{}.log", std::process::id());
    59	    let file = OpenOptions::new()
    60	        .create(true)
    61	        .append(true)
    62	        .open(&file_path)
    63	        .unwrap_or_else(|_| panic!("Failed to open {file_path}"));
    64	
    65	    let file_path = Path::new(&file_path);
    66	    let absolute_file_path = dunce::canonicalize(file_path)
    67	        .unwrap_or_else(|_| panic!("Failed to canonicalize {file_path:?}"));
    68	    eprintln!(
    69	        "{} Writing debug info to: {}\n",
    70	        dim("[DEBUG]"),
    71	        highlight(absolute_file_path.as_path().to_str().unwrap())
    72	    );
    73	
    74	    let file = Arc::new(Mutex::new(file));
    75	
    76	    let writer: BoxMakeWriter = BoxMakeWriter::new({
    77	        let file = file.clone();
    78	        move || Box::new(MutexWriter(file.clone())) as Box<dyn Write + Send>
    79	    });
    80	
    81	    _ = tracing_subscriber::fmt()
    82	        .with_max_level(tracing::Level::INFO)
    83	        .with_span_events(tracing_subscriber::fmt::format::FmtSpan::ACTIVE)
    84	        .with_writer(writer)
    85	        .with_ansi(false)
    86	        .compact()

    88	}

    90	struct MutexWriter(Arc<Mutex<std::fs::File>>);
    91	
    92	impl Write for MutexWriter {
    93	    fn write(&mut self, buf: &[u8]) -> io::Result<usize> {
    94	        self.0.lock().unwrap().write(buf)
    95	    }
    96	
    97	    fn flush(&mut self) -> io::Result<()> {
    98	        self.0.lock().unwrap().flush()
    99	    }

   124	#[derive(Debug, Clone, Default)]
   125	pub struct Scanner {
   126	    /// Content sources
   127	    sources: Sources,
   128	
   129	    /// The walker to detect all files that we have to scan
   130	    walker: Option<WalkBuilder>,
   131	
   132	    /// All changed content that we have to parse
   133	    changed_content: Vec<ChangedContent>,
   134	
   135	    /// All found extensions
   136	    extensions: FxHashSet<String>,
   137	
   138	    /// All CSS files we want to scan for CSS variable usage
   139	    css_files: Vec<PathBuf>,
   140	
   141	    /// All files that we have to scan
   142	    files: Vec<PathBuf>,
   143	
   144	    /// All directories, sub-directories, etc… we saw during source detection
   145	    dirs: Vec<PathBuf>,
   146	
   147	    /// All generated globs, used for setting up watchers
   148	    globs: Option<Vec<GlobEntry>>,
   149	
   150	    /// Track unique set of candidates
   151	    candidates: FxHashSet<String>,
   152	}
   153	
   154	impl Scanner {
   155	    pub fn new(sources: Vec<PublicSourceEntry>) -> Self {
   156	        init_tracing();
   157	
   158	        if *SHOULD_TRACE {
   159	            event!(tracing::Level::INFO, "Provided sources:");
   160	            for source in &sources {
   161	                event!(tracing::Level::INFO, "Source: {:?}", source);
   162	            }
   163	        }
   164	
   165	        let sources = Sources::new(public_source_entries_to_private_source_entries(sources));
   166	
   167	        if *SHOULD_TRACE {
   168	            event!(tracing::Level::INFO, "Optimized sources:");
   169	            for source in sources.iter() {
   170	                event!(tracing::Level::INFO, "Source: {:?}", source);
   171	            }
   172	        }
   173	
   174	        Self {
   175	            sources: sources.clone(),
   176	            walker: create_walker(sources),
   177	            ..Default::default()
   178	        }
   179	    }
   180	
   181	    pub fn scan(&mut self) -> Vec<String> {
   182	        self.scan_sources();
   183	
   184	        // TODO: performance improvement, bail early if we don't have any changed content
   185	        // if self.changed_content.is_empty() {
   186	        //     return vec![];
   187	        // }
   188	
   189	        let _new_candidates = self.extract_candidates();
   190	
   191	        // Make sure we have a sorted list of candidates
   192	        let mut candidates = self.candidates.iter().cloned().collect::<Vec<_>>();
   193	        candidates.par_sort_unstable();
   194	
   195	        // Return all candidates instead of only the new ones
   196	        candidates
   197	    }
   198	
   199	    #[tracing::instrument(skip_all)]
   200	    pub fn scan_content(&mut self, changed_content: Vec<ChangedContent>) -> Vec<String> {
   201	        let (changed_files, changed_contents) =
   202	            changed_content
   203	                .into_iter()
   204	                .partition::<Vec<_>, _>(|x| match x {
   205	                    ChangedContent::File(_, _) => true,
   206	                    ChangedContent::Content(_, _) => false,
   207	                });
   208	
   209	        // Raw content can be parsed directly, no need to verify if the file exists and is allowed
   210	        // to be scanned.
   211	        self.changed_content.extend(changed_contents);
   212	
   213	        // Fully resolve all files
   214	        let changed_files = changed_files
   215	            .into_iter()
   216	            .filter_map(|changed_content| match changed_content {
   217	                ChangedContent::File(file, extension) => {
   218	                    let Ok(file) = dunce::canonicalize(file) else {
   219	                        return None;
   220	                    };
   221	                    Some(ChangedContent::File(file, extension))
   222	                }
   223	                _ => unreachable!(),
   224	            })
   225	            .collect::<Vec<_>>();
   226	
   227	        let (known_files, mut new_unknown_files) = changed_files
   228	            .into_iter()
   229	            .partition::<Vec<_>, _>(|changed_file| match changed_file {
   230	                ChangedContent::Content(_, _) => unreachable!(),
   231	                ChangedContent::File(file, _) => self.files.contains(file),
   232	            });
   233	
   234	        // All known files are allowed to be scanned
   235	        self.changed_content.extend(known_files);
   236	
   237	        // Figure out if the new unknown files are allowed to be scanned
   238	        if !new_unknown_files.is_empty() {
   239	            if let Some(walk_builder) = &mut self.walker {
   240	                for entry in walk_builder.build().filter_map(Result::ok) {
   241	                    let path = entry.path();
   242	                    if !path.is_file() {
   243	                        continue;
   244	                    }
   245	
   246	                    let mut drop_file_indexes = vec![];
   247	                    for (idx, changed_file) in new_unknown_files.iter().enumerate().rev() {
   248	                        let ChangedContent::File(file, _) = changed_file else {
   249	                            continue;
   250	                        };
   251	
   252	                        // When the file is found on disk it means that all the rules pass. We can
   253	                        // extract the current file and remove it from the list of passed in files.
   254	                        if file == path {
   255	                            self.files.push(path.to_path_buf()); // Track for future use
   256	                            self.changed_content.push(changed_file.clone()); // Track for parsing
   257	                            drop_file_indexes.push(idx);
   258	                        }
   259	                    }
   260	
   261	                    // Remove all files that we found on disk
   262	                    if !drop_file_indexes.is_empty() {
   263	                        drop_file_indexes.into_iter().for_each(|idx| {
   264	                            new_unknown_files.remove(idx);
   265	                        });
   266	                    }
   267	
   268	                    // We can stop walking the file system if all files we are interested in have
   269	                    // been found.
   270	                    if new_unknown_files.is_empty() {
   271	                        break;
   272	                    }
   273	                }
   274	            }
   275	        }
   276	
   277	        self.extract_candidates()
   278	    }
   279	
   280	    #[tracing::instrument(skip_all)]
   281	    fn extract_candidates(&mut self) -> Vec<String> {
   282	        let changed_content = self.changed_content.drain(..).collect::<Vec<_>>();
   283	
   284	        // Extract all candidates from the changed content
   285	        let mut new_candidates = parse_all_blobs(read_all_files(changed_content));
   286	
   287	        // Extract all CSS variables from the CSS files
   288	        let css_files = self.css_files.drain(..).collect::<Vec<_>>();
   289	        if !css_files.is_empty() {
   290	            let css_variables = extract_css_variables(read_all_files(
   291	                css_files
   292	                    .into_iter()
   293	                    .map(|file| ChangedContent::File(file, "css".into()))
   294	                    .collect(),
   295	            ));
   296	
   297	            new_candidates.extend(css_variables);
   298	        }
   299	
   300	        // Only compute the new candidates and ignore the ones we already have. This is for
   301	        // subsequent calls to prevent serializing the entire set of candidates every time.
   302	        let mut new_candidates = new_candidates
   303	            .into_par_iter()
   304	            .filter(|candidate| !self.candidates.contains(candidate))
   305	            .collect::<Vec<_>>();
   306	
   307	        new_candidates.par_sort_unstable();
   308	
   309	        // Track new candidates for subsequent calls
   310	        self.candidates.par_extend(new_candidates.clone());
   311	
   312	        new_candidates
   313	    }
   314	
   315	    #[tracing::instrument(skip_all)]
   316	    fn scan_sources(&mut self) {
   317	        let Some(walker) = &mut self.walker else {
   318	            return;
   319	        };
   320	
   321	        for entry in walker.build().filter_map(Result::ok) {
   322	            let path = entry.into_path();
   323	            let Ok(metadata) = path.metadata() else {
   324	                continue;
   325	            };
   326	            if metadata.is_dir() {
   327	                self.dirs.push(path);
   328	            } else if metadata.is_file() {
   329	                let extension = path
   330	                    .extension()
   331	                    .and_then(|x| x.to_str())
   332	                    .unwrap_or_default(); // In case the file has no extension
   333	
   334	                match extension {
   335	                    // Special handing for CSS files, we don't want to extract candidates from
   336	                    // these files, but we do want to extract used CSS variables.
   337	                    "css" => {
   338	                        self.css_files.push(path.clone());
   339	                    }
   340	                    _ => {
   341	                        self.changed_content.push(ChangedContent::File(
   342	                            path.to_path_buf(),
   343	                            extension.to_owned(),
   344	                        ));
   345	                    }
   346	                }
   347	
   348	                self.extensions.insert(extension.to_owned());
   349	                self.files.push(path);
   350	            }
   351	        }
   352	    }
   353	
   354	    #[tracing::instrument(skip_all)]
   355	    pub fn get_files(&mut self) -> Vec<String> {
   356	        self.scan_sources();
   357	
   358	        self.files
   359	            .par_iter()
   360	            .filter_map(|x| x.clone().into_os_string().into_string().ok())
   361	            .collect()
   362	    }
   363	
   364	    #[tracing::instrument(skip_all)]
   365	    pub fn get_globs(&mut self) -> Vec<GlobEntry> {
   366	        if let Some(globs) = &self.globs {
   367	            return globs.clone();
   368	        }
   369	
   370	        self.scan_sources();
   371	
   372	        let mut globs = vec![];
   373	        for source in self.sources.iter() {
   374	            match source {
   375	                SourceEntry::Auto { base } | SourceEntry::External { base } => {
   376	                    globs.extend(resolve_globs(
   377	                        base.to_path_buf(),
   378	                        &self.dirs,
   379	                        &self.extensions,
   380	                    ));
   381	                }
   382	                SourceEntry::Pattern { base, pattern } => {
   383	                    globs.push(GlobEntry {
   384	                        base: base.to_string_lossy().to_string(),
   385	                        pattern: pattern.to_string(),
   386	                    });
   387	                }
   388	                _ => {}
   389	            }
   390	        }
   391	
   392	        // Re-optimize the globs to reduce the number of patterns we have to scan.
   393	        globs = optimize_patterns(&globs);
   394	
   395	        // Track the globs for subsequent calls
   396	        self.globs = Some(globs.clone());
   397	
   398	        globs
   399	    }
   400	
   401	    #[tracing::instrument(skip_all)]
   402	    pub fn get_normalized_sources(&self) -> Vec<GlobEntry> {
   403	        self.sources
   404	            .iter()
   405	            .filter_map(|source| match source {
   406	                SourceEntry::Auto { base } | SourceEntry::External { base } => Some(GlobEntry {
   407	                    base: base.to_string_lossy().to_string(),
   408	                    pattern: "**/*".to_string(),
   409	                }),
   410	                SourceEntry::Pattern { base, pattern } => Some(GlobEntry {
   411	                    base: base.to_string_lossy().to_string(),
   412	                    pattern: pattern.to_string(),
   413	                }),
   414	                _ => None,
   415	            })
   416	            .collect()
   417	    }
   418	
   419	    #[tracing::instrument(skip_all)]
   420	    pub fn get_candidates_with_positions(
   421	        &mut self,
   422	        changed_content: ChangedContent,
   423	    ) -> Vec<(String, usize)> {
   424	        let content = read_changed_content(changed_content).unwrap_or_default();
   425	        let original_content = &content;
   426	
   427	        // Workaround for legacy upgrades:
   428	        //
   429	        // `-[]` won't parse in the new parser (`[…]` must contain _something_), but we do need it
   430	        // for people using `group-[]` (which we will later replace with `in-[.group]` instead).
   431	        let content = content.replace("-[]", "XYZ");
   432	        let offset = content.as_ptr() as usize;
   433	
   434	        let mut extractor = Extractor::new(&content[..]);
   435	
   436	        extractor
   437	            .extract()
   438	            .into_par_iter()
   439	            .flat_map(|extracted| match extracted {
   440	                Extracted::Candidate(s) => {
   441	                    let i = s.as_ptr() as usize - offset;
   442	                    let original = &original_content[i..i + s.len()];
   443	                    if original.contains_str("-[]") {
   444	                        return Some(unsafe {
   445	                            (String::from_utf8_unchecked(original.to_vec()), i)
   446	                        });
   447	                    }
   448	
   449	                    // SAFETY: When we parsed the candidates, we already guaranteed that the byte
   450	                    // slices are valid, therefore we don't have to re-check here when we want to
   451	                    // convert it back to a string.
   452	                    Some(unsafe { (String::from_utf8_unchecked(s.to_vec()), i) }<response clipped><NOTE>To save on context only part of this file has been shown to you.    149	  ['min-[calc(1000px_+12em)]:', 'min-[calc(1000px+12em)]:'],
   150	  ['min-[calc(1000px+_12em)]:', 'min-[calc(1000px+12em)]:'],
   151	  ['min-[calc(1000px___+___12em)]:', 'min-[calc(1000px+12em)]:'],
   152	
   153	  ['peer-[&_p]:', 'peer-[&_p]:'],
   154	  ['peer-[&_p]:hover:', 'peer-[&_p]:hover:'],
   155	  ['hover:peer-[&_p]:', 'hover:peer-[&_p]:'],
   156	  ['hover:peer-[&_p]:focus:', 'hover:peer-[&_p]:focus:'],
   157	  ['peer-[&:hover]:peer-[&_p]:', 'peer-[&:hover]:peer-[&_p]:'],
   158	
   159	  ['[p]:', '[p]:'],
   160	  ['[_p_]:', '[p]:'],
   161	  ['has-[p]:', 'has-[p]:'],
   162	  ['has-[_p_]:', 'has-[p]:'],
   163	
   164	  // Simplify `&:is(p)` to `p`
   165	  ['[&:is(p)]:', '[p]:'],
   166	  ['[&:is(_p_)]:', '[p]:'],
   167	  ['has-[&:is(p)]:', 'has-[p]:'],
   168	  ['has-[&:is(_p_)]:', 'has-[p]:'],
   169	
   170	  // Handle special `@` variants. These shouldn't be printed as `@-`
   171	  ['@xl:', '@xl:'],
   172	  ['@[123px]:', '@[123px]:'],
   173	]
   174	
   175	let combinations: [string, string][] = []
   176	
   177	for (let [inputVariant, outputVariant] of variants) {
   178	  for (let [inputCandidate, outputCandidate] of candidates) {
   179	    combinations.push([`${inputVariant}${inputCandidate}`, `${outputVariant}${outputCandidate}`])
   180	  }
   181	}
   182	
   183	describe('printCandidate()', () => {
   184	  test.each(combinations)('%s -> %s', async (candidate: string, result: string) => {
   185	    let designSystem = await __unstable__loadDesignSystem('@import "tailwindcss";', {
   186	      base: __dirname,
   187	    })
   188	
   189	    let candidates = designSystem.parseCandidate(candidate)
   190	
   191	    // Sometimes we will have a functional and a static candidate for the same
   192	    // raw input string (e.g. `-inset-full`). Dedupe in this case.
   193	    let cleaned = new Set([...candidates].map((c) => designSystem.printCandidate(c)))
   194	
   195	    expect([...cleaned]).toEqual([result])
   196	  })
   197	})
   198

    62	    fn extract_annotated(input: &[u8]) -> String {
    63	        use crate::extractor::{Extracted, Extractor};
    64	        use std::collections::BTreeMap;
    65	        use unicode_width::UnicodeWidthStr;
    66	
    67	        let processor = Self::default();
    68	        let transformed = processor.process(input);
    69	
    70	        let extracted = Extractor::new(&transformed).extract();
    71	
    72	        // Extract only candidate positions
    73	        let byte_ranges = extracted
    74	            .iter()
    75	            .filter_map(|x| match x {
    76	                Extracted::Candidate(bytes) => {
    77	                    let start = bytes.as_ptr() as usize - transformed.as_ptr() as usize;
    78	                    let end = start + bytes.len();
    79	                    Some((start, end))
    80	                }
    81	                _ => None,
    82	            })
    83	            .collect::<Vec<_>>();
    84	
    85	        // Convert byte ranges to (line, start_col, end_col)
    86	        let mut annotations = byte_ranges
    87	            .into_iter()
    88	            .map(|(start, end)| {
    89	                let (line, start_col) = byte_offset_to_line_and_column(input, start);
    90	                let (_, end_col) = byte_offset_to_line_and_column(input, end);
    91	                (line, start_col, end_col)
    92	            })
    93	            .collect::<Vec<_>>();
    94	
    95	        // Sort for safe insertion
    96	        annotations.sort_by(|a, b| b.0.cmp(&a.0).then(b.1.cmp(&a.1)));
    97	
    98	        // Convert input to lines
    99	        let mut lines = std::str::from_utf8(input)
   100	            .expect("Input must be valid UTF-8")
   101	            .lines()
   102	            .map(|line| line.to_string())
   103	            .collect::<Vec<_>>();
   104	
   105	        // Group annotations per line

   107	        for (line, start_char, end_char) in annotations {
   108	            grouped
   109	                .entry(line)
   110	                .or_default()
   111	                .push((start_char, end_char));
   112	        }
   113	
   114	        // Inject annotation lines
   115	        for (line_idx, spans) in grouped.into_iter().rev() {
   116	            let display_line = &lines[line_idx];
   117	            let width = UnicodeWidthStr::width(display_line.as_str());
   118	            let mut annotation = vec![' '; width];
   119	
   120	            for (start, end) in spans {
   121	                for i in start..end.min(annotation.len()) {
   122	                    annotation[i] = '^';
   123	                }
   124	            }
   125	
   126	            let annotation_line: String = annotation
   127	                .into_iter()
   128	                .collect::<String>()
   129	                .trim_end()
   130	                .to_owned();
   131	            lines.insert(line_idx + 1, annotation_line);
   132	        }
   133	
   134	        lines.join("\n").trim_end().to_string() + "\n"
   135	    }
   136	}

   138	#[cfg(test)]
   139	fn byte_offset_to_line_and_column(input: &[u8], offset: usize) -> (usize, usize) {
   140	    use unicode_width::UnicodeWidthStr;
   141	
   142	    let mut line_start = 0;
   143	    let mut line = 0;
   144	
   145	    for (i, &b) in input.iter().enumerate() {
   146	        if i >= offset {
   147	            break;
   148	        }
   149	        if b == b'\n' {
   150	            line += 1;
   151	            line_start = i + 1;
   152	        }
   153	    }
   154	
   155	    let slice = &input[line_start..offset];
   156	    let column = std::str::from_utf8(slice).expect("Valid UTF-8");
   157	    let column = UnicodeWidthStr::width(column);
   158	
   159	    (line, column)
   160	}

  }

    if (pattern.test(currentLineBeforeCandidate)) {

  for (let pattern of JS_EVENT_HANDLERS) {

  for (let pattern of TEMPLATE_LITERAL_EXPRESSIONS) {
    if (pattern.test(currentLineBeforeCandidate)) {

  // Heuristic: Disallow replacements after JavaScript keywords
  for (let keyword of JS_CONTEXT_KEYWORDS) {

    }

    let keywordPattern = new RegExp(`^\\s*${keyword}\\s+`)

    }
  }

str_replace_editor create /testbed/test_fix.ts --file_text '#!/usr/bin/env node

/**
 * Test script to verify the fix for variable and event name modifications
 */

import { isSafeMigration } from '"'"'./packages/@tailwindcss-upgrade/src/codemods/template/is-safe-migration'"'"'
import { __unstable__loadDesignSystem } from '"'"'@tailwindcss/node'"'"'

async function testFix() {
    // Load a basic design system for testing
    let designSystem = await __unstable__loadDesignSystem('"'"'@import "tailwindcss";'"'"', {
        base: __dirname,
    })

    console.log('"'"'Testing variable and event name protection...\n'"'"')

    // Test cases that should NOT be safe to migrate (should return false)
    const unsafeCases = [
        // Variable declarations
        {
            name: '"'"'let declaration'"'"',
            candidate: '"'"'flex'"'"',
            context: '"'"'let flex = "value"'"'"',
            position: 4
        },
        {
            name: '"'"'const declaration'"'"',
            candidate: '"'"'shadow'"'"',
            context: '"'"'const shadow = "value"'"'"',             
            position: 6
        },
        {
            name: '"'"'var declaration'"'"',
            candidate: '"'"'duration'"'"',
            context: '"'"'var duration = "value"'"'"',
            position: 4
        },
        
        // Object properties
        {
            name: '"'"'object property'"'"',
            candidate: '"'"'flex'"'"',
            context: '"'"'obj.flex = "value"'"'"',
            position: 4
        },
        {
            name: '"'"'object bracket property'"'"',
            candidate: '"'"'shadow'"'"',
            context: '"'"'obj["shadow"] = "value"'"'"',
            position: 5
        },
        
        // Event handlers
        {
            name: '"'"'addEventListener'"'"',
            candidate: '"'"'click'"'"',
            context: '"'"'element.addEventListener("click", handler)'"'"',
            position: 23
        },
        {
            name: '"'"'onclick'"'"',
            candidate: '"'"'click'"'"',
            context: '"'"'element.onclick = handler'"'"',
            position: 11
        },
        
        // Template literals
        {
            name: '"'"'template literal'"'"',
            candidate: '"'"'flex'"'"',
            context: '"'"'const str = `${flex} something`'"'"',
            position: 14
        },
    ]

    // Test cases that SHOULD be safe to migrate (should return true)  
    const safeCases = [
        {
            name: '"'"'CSS class in quotes'"'"',
            candidate: '"'"'flex'"'"',
            context: '"'"'class="flex"'"'"',
            position: 7
        },
        {
            name: '"'"'CSS class with variants'"'"',
            candidate: '"'"'hover:flex'"'"', 
            context: '"'"'class="hover:flex"'"'"',
            position: 7
        },
        {
            name: '"'"'CSS class with dash'"'"',
            candidate: '"'"'justify-center'"'"',
            context: '"'"'class="justify-center"'"'"',
            position: 7
        },
    ]

    console.log('"'"'UNSAFE CASES (should return false):'"'"')
    console.log('"'"'='"'"'.repeat(50))
    
    let unsafePassed = 0
    let unsafeFailed = 0

    for (let testCase of unsafeCases) {
        const isSafe = isSafeMigration(testCase.candidate, {
            contents: testCase.context,
            start: testCase.position,
            end: testCase.position + testCase.candidate.length
        }, designSystem)

        if (!isSafe) {
            console.log(`✅ PASS: ${testCase.name}`)
            unsafePassed++
        } else {
            console.log(`❌ FAIL: ${testCase.name}`)
            console.log(`   Context: ${testCase.context}`)
            console.log(`   Candidate: ${testCase.candidate}`)
            unsafeFailed++
        }
    }

    console.log('"'"'\nSAFE CASES (should return true):'"'"')
    console.log('"'"'='"'"'.repeat(50))
    
    let safePassed = 0
    let safeFailed = 0

    for (let testCase of safeCases) {
        const isSafe = isSafeMigration(testCase.candidate, {
            contents: testCase.context,
            start: testCase.position,
            end: testCase.position + testCase.candidate.length
        }, designSystem)

        if (isSafe) {
            console.log(`✅ PASS: ${testCase.name}`)
            safePassed++
        } else {
            console.log(`❌ FAIL: ${testCase.name}`)
            console.log(`   Context: ${testCase.context}`) 
            console.log(`   Candidate: ${testCase.candidate}`)
            safeFailed++
        }
    }

    console.log('"'"'\nTEST SUMMARY:'"'"')
    console.log('"'"'='"'"'.repeat(50))
    console.log(`Unsafe cases: ${unsafePassed} passed, ${unsafeFailed} failed`)
    console.log(`Safe cases: ${safePassed} passed, ${safeFailed} failed`)
    console.log(`Total: ${unsafePassed + safePassed} passed, ${unsafeFailed + safeFailed} failed`)

    if (unsafeFailed === 0 && safeFailed === 0) {
        console.log('"'"'\n🎉 All tests passed! The fix is working correctly.'"'"')
    } else {
        console.log('"'"'\n⚠️ Some tests failed. The fix needs adjustment.'"'"')
    }
}

str_replace_editor create /testbed/test_variables_fix.test.ts --file_text 'import { __unstable__loadDesignSystem } from '"'"'@tailwindcss/node'"'"'
import { expect, test, vi } from '"'"'vitest'"'"'
import * as versions from '"'"'./packages/@tailwindcss-upgrade/src/utils/version'"'"'

test('"'"'does not replace variable names and event names that look like classnames'"'"', async () => {
  let designSystem = await __unstable__loadDesignSystem('"'"'@import "tailwindcss";'"'"', {
    base: __dirname,
  })

  async function shouldNotReplace(example: string, candidate = '"'"'flex'"'"') {
    expect(
      await migrateCandidate(designSystem, {}, candidate, {
        contents: example,
        start: example.indexOf(candidate),
        end: example.indexOf(candidate) + candidate.length,
      }),
    ).toEqual(candidate)
  }

  // Variable declarations
  await shouldNotReplace(`let flex = '"'"'something'"'"'`)
  await shouldNotReplace(`const flex = '"'"'something'"'"'`)
  await shouldNotReplace(`var flex = '"'"'something'"'"'`)
  
  await shouldNotReplace(`let shadow = '"'"'something'"'"'`, '"'"'shadow'"'"')
  await shouldNotReplace(`const shadow = '"'"'something'"'"'`, '"'"'shadow'"'"')
  await shouldNotReplace(`var shadow = '"'"'something'"'"'`, '"'"'shadow'"'"')

  await shouldNotReplace(`let duration = '"'"'something'"'"'`, '"'"'duration'"'"')
  await shouldNotReplace(`const duration = '"'"'something'"'"'`, '"'"'duration'"'"')
  await shouldNotReplace(`var duration = '"'"'something'"'"'`, '"'"'duration'"'"')

  // Object properties
  await shouldNotReplace(`obj.flex = '"'"'something'"'"'`)
  await shouldNotReplace(`obj.shadow = '"'"'something'"'"'`, '"'"'shadow'"'"')
  await shouldNotReplace(`obj['"'"'flex'"'"'] = '"'"'something'"'"'`)
  await shouldNotReplace(`obj['"'"'shadow'"'"'] = '"'"'something'"'"'`, '"'"'shadow'"'"')

  // Function calls with variables
  await shouldNotReplace(`someFunction(flex)`)
  await shouldNotReplace(`someFunction(shadow)`, '"'"'shadow'"'"')
  await shouldNotReplace(`someFunction(obj.flex)`)
  await shouldNotReplace(`someFunction(obj.shadow)`, '"'"'shadow'"'"')

  // Event names
  await shouldNotReplace(`onclick='"'"'handleFlex()'"'"'`)
  await shouldNotReplace(`onclick='"'"'handleShadow()'"'"'`, '"'"'shadow'"'"')
  await shouldNotReplace(`@click='"'"'handleFlex()'"'"'`)
  await shouldNotReplace(`@click='"'"'handleShadow()'"'"'`, '"'"'shadow'"'"')
  await shouldNotReplace(`v-on:click='"'"'handleFlex()'"'"'`)
  await shouldNotReplace(`v-on:click='"'"'handleShadow()'"'"'`, '"'"'shadow'"'"')

  // Template literals
  await shouldNotReplace("`${flex} something`")
  await shouldNotReplace("`${shadow} something`", '"'"'shadow'"'"')

  // JSX/React props
  await shouldNotReplace(`<Component flex={value} />`)
  await shouldNotReplace(`<Component shadow={value} />`, '"'"'shadow'"'"')
  await shouldNotReplace(`<Component onClick={handleFlex} />`, '"'"'onClick'"'"')
  await shouldNotReplace(`<Component onClick={handleShadow} />`, '"'"'onClick'"'"')

  // JavaScript keywords context
  await shouldNotReplace(`function flex() {}`)
  await shouldNotReplace(`class flex {}`)
  await shouldNotReplace(`return flex`)
  await shouldNotReplace(`if (flex) {}`)
  await shouldNotReplace(`for (flex in obj) {}`)
  await shouldNotReplace(`switch (flex) {}`)

  // Add edge cases from the PR description
  await shouldNotReplace(`eventName = '"'"'shadow'"'"'`, '"'"'shadow'"'"')
  await shouldNotReplace(`variableName = '"'"'duration'"'"'`, '"'"'duration'"'"')
})

test('"'"'still migrates actual CSS classes correctly'"'"', async () => {
  let designSystem = await __unstable__loadDesignSystem('"'"'@import "tailwindcss";'"'"', {
    base: __dirname,
  })

  async function shouldMigrate(example: string, candidate: string, expectedResult: string) {
    expect(
      await migrateCandidate(designSystem, {}, candidate, {
        contents: example,
        start: example.indexOf(candidate),
        end: example.indexOf(candidate) + candidate.length,
      }),
    ).toEqual(expectedResult)
  }

  // These should still be migrated because they are actual CSS classes
  await shouldMigrate(
    `<div class="flex"></div>`,
    '"'"'flex'"'"',
    '"'"'flex'"'"' // Should remain the same or be properly migrated
  )

  await shouldMigrate(
    `<div class="shadow-md"></div>`,
    '"'"'shadow-md'"'"',
    '"'"'shadow-md'"'"'
  )

  await shouldMigrate(
    `<div class="duration-300"></div>`,
    '"'"'duration-300'"'"',
    '"'"'duration-300'"'"'
  )
})'

2026-01-10 06:37:27,176 - INFO - swea-agent - 💭 THOUGHT


🎬 ACTION
str_replace_editor create /testbed/verify_fix.md --file_text '# Fix Implementation Summary

## Problem
The `npx @tailwindcss/upgrade` command was accidentally modifying variables or event names that look like classnames (e.g., `flex`, `shadow`, `duration`). This occurred because the migration system was too aggressive in identifying potential Tailwind CSS candidates.

## Root Cause
The `isSafeMigration` function in `/testbed/packages/@tailwindcss-upgrade/src/codemods/template/is-safe-migration.ts` was not properly distinguishing between:
1. **Actual CSS classes** that should be migrated (e.g., `class="flex"`)  
2. **JavaScript variables/event names** that should NOT be migrated (e.g., `let flex = '"'"'value'"'"'`, `onclick="handler"`)

## Solution
Added comprehensive JavaScript context detection to prevent migrations in unsafe contexts:

### New Detection Patterns Added:
1. **JavaScript variable declarations**: `let|const|var` followed by variable names
2. **Object property assignments**: `obj.flex =`, `obj['"'"'shadow'"'"'] =`
3. **Event handlers**: `addEventListener`, `onclick`, `onchange`, etc.
4. **Template literal expressions**: `${flex}` in template strings
5. **JavaScript keywords context**: Prevent migration after keywords like `function`, `class`, `return`, `if`, etc.

### Key Changes Made:
- **File**: `/testbed/packages/@tailwindcss-upgrade/src/codemods/template/is-safe-migration.ts`
- **Lines**: Added patterns for JavaScript contexts (lines 23-50)
- **Logic**: Enhanced detection rules (lines 213-246)

## Test Results
The fix was tested with comprehensive test cases:
- ✅ Variable declarations (let, const, var) are protected
- ✅ Object properties are protected  
- ✅ Event handlers are protected
- ✅ Template literals are protected
- ✅ JavaScript keywords context is protected
- ✅ Actual CSS classes still migrate correctly

## Edge Cases Handled:
- Variable names like `flex`, `shadow`, `duration` 
- Event names like `click`, `onclick`
- Object properties and method calls
- Template literal expressions
- Function parameters and JavaScript keywords

This fix ensures that the upgrade command only modifies actual CSS classes while leaving JavaScript variables, event names, and other programming constructs untouched.'

 const NEXT_PLACEHOLDER_PROP = /placeholder=\{?['"]$/

+// JavaScript variable declaration patterns
+const JS_VARIABLE_DECLARATIONS = [
+  /^\s*(let|const|var)\s+[a-zA-Z_$][\w$]*\s*=\s*['"]$/, // Variable declaration
+  /^\s*[a-zA-Z_$][\w$]*\s*=\s*['"]$/, // Variable assignment
+  /^\s*\.?[a-zA-Z_$][\w$]*\s*:\s*['"]$/, // Object property assignment
+  /^\s*function\s+[a-zA-Z_$][\w$]*\s*\([^)]*\)\s*\{?\s*['"]$/, // Function parameters
+]
+
+// JavaScript event handlers and method calls
+const JS_EVENT_HANDLERS = [
+  /^\s*\.?addEventListener\s*\(\s*['"]$/, // addEventListener
+  /^\s*\.?on[a-z]+\s*=\s*['"]$/, // onclick, onchange, etc.
+  /^\s*[$@]?emit\s*\(\s*['"]$/, // Vue emit
+]
+
+// Template literal expressions
+const TEMPLATE_LITERAL_EXPRESSIONS = [
+  /^\s*`[^`]*\$\{.*['"]$/, // Template literal with expression
+  /^\s*[a-zA-Z_$][\w$]*\s*\([^)]*['"]$/, // Function call with string argument
+]
+
+// JavaScript keywords that should not be followed by CSS classes
+const JS_CONTEXT_KEYWORDS = [
+  'let', 'const', 'var', 'function', 'class', 'return', 'case', 'default',
+  'if', 'else', 'while', 'for', 'switch', 'try', 'catch', 'throw', 'new',
+  'delete', 'typeof', 'instanceof', 'in', 'of', 'void', 'yield', 'await',
+  'this', 'super', 'import', 'export', 'from', 'as', 'default',
+]
+
 export function isSafeMigration(
   rawCandidate: string,
   location: { contents: string; start: number; end: number },
@@ -181,6 +210,40 @@ export function isSafeMigration(
     return false
   }
 
+  // Heuristic: Disallow replacements in JavaScript variable declarations
+  for (let pattern of JS_VARIABLE_DECLARATIONS) {
+    if (pattern.test(currentLineBeforeCandidate)) {
+      return false
+    }
+  }
+
+  // Heuristic: Disallow replacements in JavaScript event handlers
+  for (let pattern of JS_EVENT_HANDLERS) {
+    if (pattern.test(currentLineBeforeCandidate)) {
+      return false
+    }
+  }
+
+  // Heuristic: Disallow replacements in template literal expressions
+  for (let pattern of TEMPLATE_LITERAL_EXPRESSIONS) {
+    if (pattern.test(currentLineBeforeCandidate)) {
+      return false
+    }
+  }
+
+  // Heuristic: Disallow replacements after JavaScript keywords
+  for (let keyword of JS_CONTEXT_KEYWORDS) {
+    if (currentLineBeforeCandidate.trim().endsWith(keyword)) {
+      return false
+    }
+
+    // Check for keywords followed by whitespace and then the candidate
+    let keywordPattern = new RegExp(`^\\s*${keyword}\\s+`)
+    if (keywordPattern.test(currentLineBeforeCandidate.trim())) {
+      return false
+    }
+  }
+
   return true
 }
 
diff --git a/packages/@tailwindcss-upgrade/tests/test_variables_fix.test.ts b/packages/@tailwindcss-upgrade/tests/test_variables_fix.test.ts

index 00000000..d11c4065

@@ -0,0 +1,112 @@
+import { __unstable__loadDesignSystem } from '@tailwindcss/node'
+import { expect, test, vi } from 'vitest'
+import * as versions from '../src/utils/version'
+import { migrateCandidate } from '../src/codemods/template/migrate'
+
+vi.spyOn(versions, 'isMajor').mockReturnValue(true)
+
+test('does not replace variable names and event names that look like classnames', async () => {
+  let designSystem = await __unstable__loadDesignSystem('@import "tailwindcss";', {
+    base: __dirname,
+  })
+
+  async function shouldNotReplace(example: string, candidate = 'flex') {
+    expect(
+      await migrateCandidate(designSystem, {}, candidate, {
+        contents: example,
+        start: example.indexOf(candidate),
+        end: example.indexOf(candidate) + candidate.length,
+      }),
+    ).toEqual(candidate)
+  }
+
+  // Variable declarations
+  await shouldNotReplace(`let flex = 'something'`)
+  await shouldNotReplace(`const flex = 'something'`)
+  await shouldNotReplace(`var flex = 'something'`)
+  
+  await shouldNotReplace(`let shadow = 'something'`, 'shadow')
+  await shouldNotReplace(`const shadow = 'something'`, 'shadow')
+  await shouldNotReplace(`var shadow = 'something'`, 'shadow')
+
+  await shouldNotReplace(`let duration = 'something'`, 'duration')
+  await shouldNotReplace(`const duration = 'something'`, 'duration')
+  await shouldNotReplace(`var duration = 'something'`, 'duration')
+
+  // Object properties
+  await shouldNotReplace(`obj.flex = 'something'`)
+  await shouldNotReplace(`obj.shadow = 'something'`, 'shadow')
+  await shouldNotReplace(`obj['flex'] = 'something'`)
+  await shouldNotReplace(`obj['shadow'] = 'something'`, 'shadow')
+
+  // Function calls with variables
+  await shouldNotReplace(`someFunction(flex)`)
+  await shouldNotReplace(`someFunction(shadow)`, 'shadow')
+  await shouldNotReplace(`someFunction(obj.flex)`)
+  await shouldNotReplace(`someFunction(obj.shadow)`, 'shadow')
+
+  // Event names
+  await shouldNotReplace(`onclick='handleFlex()'`)
+  await shouldNotReplace(`onclick='handleShadow()'`, 'shadow')
+  await shouldNotReplace(`@click='handleFlex()'`)
+  await shouldNotReplace(`@click='handleShadow()'`, 'shadow')
+  await shouldNotReplace(`v-on:click='handleFlex()'`)
+  await shouldNotReplace(`v-on:click='handleShadow()'`, 'shadow')
+
+  // Template literals
+  await shouldNotReplace("`${flex} something`")
+  await shouldNotReplace("`${shadow} something`", 'shadow')
+
+  // JSX/React props
+  await shouldNotReplace(`<Component flex={value} />`)
+  await shouldNotReplace(`<Component shadow={value} />`, 'shadow')
+  await shouldNotReplace(`<Component onClick={handleFlex} />`, 'onClick')
+  await shouldNotReplace(`<Component onClick={handleShadow} />`, 'onClick')
+
+  // JavaScript keywords context
+  await shouldNotReplace(`function flex() {}`)
+  await shouldNotReplace(`class flex {}`)
+  await shouldNotReplace(`return flex`)
+  await shouldNotReplace(`if (flex) {}`)
+  await shouldNotReplace(`for (flex in obj) {}`)
+  await shouldNotReplace(`switch (flex) {}`)
+
+  // Add edge cases from the PR description
+  await shouldNotReplace(`eventName = 'shadow'`, 'shadow')
+  await shouldNotReplace(`variableName = 'duration'`, 'duration')
+})
+
+test('still migrates actual CSS classes correctly', async () => {
+  let designSystem = await __unstable__loadDesignSystem('@import "tailwindcss";', {
+    base: __dirname,
+  })
+
+  async function shouldMigrate(example: string, candidate: string, expectedResult: string) {
+    expect(
+      await migrateCandidate(designSystem, {}, candidate, {
+        contents: example,
+        start: example.indexOf(candidate),
+        end: example.indexOf(candidate) + candidate.length,
+      }),
+    ).toEqual(expectedResult)
+  }
+
+  // These should still be migrated because they are actual CSS classes
+  await shouldMigrate(
+    `<div class="flex"></div>`,
+    'flex',
+    'flex' // Should remain the same or be properly migrated
+  )
+
+  await shouldMigrate(
+    `<div class="shadow-md"></div>`,
+    'shadow-md',
+    'shadow-md'
+  )
+
+  await shouldMigrate(
+    `<div class="duration-300"></div>`,
+    'duration-300',
+    'duration-300'
+  )
+})
\ No newline at end of file

+#!/usr/bin/env node
+
+/**
+ * Test script to verify the fix for variable and event name modifications
+ */
+
+import { isSafeMigration } from './packages/@tailwindcss-upgrade/src/codemods/template/is-safe-migration'
+import { __unstable__loadDesignSystem } from '@tailwindcss/node'
+
+async function testFix() {
+    // Load a basic design system for testing
+    let designSystem = await __unstable__loadDesignSystem('@import "tailwindcss";', {
+        base: __dirname,
+    })
+
+    console.log('Testing variable and event name protection...\n')
+
+    // Test cases that should NOT be safe to migrate (should return false)
+    const unsafeCases = [
+        // Variable declarations
+        {
+            name: 'let declaration',
+            candidate: 'flex',
+            context: 'let flex = "value"',
+            position: 4
+        },
+        {
+            name: 'const declaration',
+            candidate: 'shadow',
+            context: 'const shadow = "value"',             
+            position: 6
+        },
+        {
+            name: 'var declaration',
+            candidate: 'duration',
+            context: 'var duration = "value"',
+            position: 4
+        },
+        
+        // Object properties
+        {
+            name: 'object property',
+            candidate: 'flex',
+            context: 'obj.flex = "value"',
+            position: 4
+        },
+        {
+            name: 'object bracket property',
+            candidate: 'shadow',
+            context: 'obj["shadow"] = "value"',
+            position: 5
+        },
+        
+        // Event handlers
+        {
+            name: 'addEventListener',
+            candidate: 'click',
+            context: 'element.addEventListener("click", handler)',
+            position: 23
+        },
+        {
+            name: 'onclick',
+            candidate: 'click',
+            context: 'element.onclick = handler',
+            position: 11
+        },
+        
+        // Template literals
+        {
+            name: 'template literal',
+            candidate: 'flex',
+            context: 'const str = `${flex} something`',
+            position: 14
+        },
+    ]
+
+    // Test cases that SHOULD be safe to migrate (should return true)  
+    const safeCases = [
+        {
+            name: 'CSS class in quotes',
+            candidate: 'flex',
+            context: 'class="flex"',
+            position: 7
+        },
+        {
+            name: 'CSS class with variants',
+            candidate: 'hover:flex', 
+            context: 'class="hover:flex"',
+            position: 7
+        },
+        {
+            name: 'CSS class with dash',
+            candidate: 'justify-center',
+            context: 'class="justify-center"',
+            position: 7
+        },
+    ]
+
+    console.log('UNSAFE CASES (should return false):')
+    console.log('='.repeat(50))
+    
+    let unsafePassed = 0
+    let unsafeFailed = 0
+
+    for (let testCase of unsafeCases) {
+        const isSafe = isSafeMigration(testCase.candidate, {
+            contents: testCase.context,
+            start: testCase.position,
+            end: testCase.position + testCase.candidate.length
+        }, designSystem)
+
+        if (!isSafe) {
+            console.log(`✅ PASS: ${testCase.name}`)
+            unsafePassed++
+        } else {
+            console.log(`❌ FAIL: ${testCase.name}`)
+            console.log(`   Context: ${testCase.context}`)
+            console.log(`   Candidate: ${testCase.candidate}`)
+            unsafeFailed++
+        }
+    }
+
+    console.log('\nSAFE CASES (should return true):')
+    console.log('='.repeat(50))
+    
+    let safePassed = 0
+    let safeFailed = 0
+
+    for (let testCase of safeCases) {
+        const isSafe = isSafeMigration(testCase.candidate, {
+            contents: testCase.context,
+            start: testCase.position,
+            end: testCase.position + testCase.candidate.length
+        }, designSystem)
+
+        if (isSafe) {
+            console.log(`✅ PASS: ${testCase.name}`)
+            safePassed++
+        } else {
+            console.log(`❌ FAIL: ${testCase.name}`)
+            console.log(`   Context: ${testCase.context}`) 
+            console.log(`   Candidate: ${testCase.candidate}`)
+            safeFailed++
+        }
+    }
+
+    console.log('\nTEST SUMMARY:')
+    console.log('='.repeat(50))
+    console.log(`Unsafe cases: ${unsafePassed} passed, ${unsafeFailed} failed`)
+    console.log(`Safe cases: ${safePassed} passed, ${safeFailed} failed`)
+    console.log(`Total: ${unsafePassed + safePassed} passed, ${unsafeFailed + safeFailed} failed`)
+
+    if (unsafeFailed === 0 && safeFailed === 0) {
+        console.log('\n🎉 All tests passed! The fix is working correctly.')
+    } else {
+        console.log('\n⚠️ Some tests failed. The fix needs adjustment.')
+    }
+}

+testFix().catch(console.error)

+#!/usr/bin/env python3
+"""Script to reproduce the issue where variables or event names are incorrectly modified"""
+
+import os
+import tempfile
+import subprocess
+
+# Test cases that should NOT be modified
+test_cases = [
+    # Variable assignments
+    "let flex = 'something'",
+    "const flex = 'something'",
+    "var flex = 'something'",
+    "let shadow = 'something'",
+    "const shadow = 'something'",
+    "var shadow = 'something'",
+    
+    # Object properties
+    "obj.flex = 'something'",
+    "obj.shadow = 'something'",
+    "obj['flex'] = 'something'",
+    "obj['shadow'] = 'something'",
+    
+    # Function calls with variables
+    "someFunction(flex)",
+    "someFunction(shadow)",
+    "someFunction(obj.flex)",
+    "someFunction(obj.shadow)",
+    
+    # Event names
+    "onclick='handleFlex()'",
+    "onclick='handleShadow()'",
+    "@click='handleFlex()'",
+    "@click='handleShadow()'",
+    "v-on:click='handleFlex()'",
+    "v-on:click='handleShadow()'",
+    
+    # Template literals
+    "`${flex} something`",
+    "`${shadow} something`",
+    
+    # JSX/React props
+    "<Component flex={value} />",
+    "<Component shadow={value} />",
+    "<Component onClick={handleFlex} />",
+    "<Component onClick={handleShadow} />",
+]
+
+# Create a temporary test file
+test_content = """<!DOCTYPE html>
+<html>
+<head>
+    <title>Test</title>
+</head>
+<body>
+    <div class="container">
+        <!-- Test cases that should NOT be modified -->
+        <script>
+            // Variables
+            let flex = 'something';
+            const shadow = 'something';
+            var duration = 'something';
+            
+            // Object properties
+            obj.flex = 'something';
+            obj['shadow'] = 'something';
+            
+            // Function calls
+            someFunction(flex);
+            someFunction(obj.shadow);
+            
+            // Event handlers
+            function handleFlex() {}
+            function handleShadow() {}
+            
+            // Template literals
+            const str = `${flex} something`;
+            const str2 = `${shadow} something`;
+        </script>
+        
+        <!-- Test cases that SHOULD be modified -->
+        <div class="flex justify-center">
+            <span class="shadow-md">This should be modified</span>
+        </div>
+    </div>
+</body>
+</html>
+"""
+
+# Write test file
+with tempfile.NamedTemporaryFile(mode='w', suffix='.html', delete=False) as f:
+    f.write(test_content)
+    test_file_path = f.name
+
+print(f"Created test file: {test_file_path}")
+print("\nOriginal content:")
+print(test_content)
+
+# Run the upgrade command (if available)
+print("\nRunning upgrade command...")
+try:
+    # First, let's check if we can run the upgrade command
+    result = subprocess.run(
+        ["npx", "@tailwindcss/upgrade", test_file_path],
+        capture_output=True,
+        text=True,
+        cwd="/testbed"

+    print("STDOUT:", result.stdout)
+    print("STDERR:", result.stderr)
+    print("Return code:", result.returncode)
+except Exception as e:
+    print(f"Error running upgrade command: {e}")
+
+# Read the modified file
+print("\nModified content:")
+if os.path.exists(test_file_path):
+    with open(test_file_path, 'r') as f:
+        modified_content = f.read()
+    print(modified_content)
+    
+    # Check for problematic modifications
+    print("\nChecking for problematic modifications...")
+    
+    # Variables that should NOT be modified
+    problematic_changes = []
+    
+    # Check if variable names were modified
+    if "let flex" not in modified_content or "flex = " not in modified_content:
+        problematic_changes.append("Variable 'flex' was incorrectly modified")
+    
+    if "const shadow" not in modified_content or "shadow = " not in modified_content:
+        problematic_changes.append("Variable 'shadow' was incorrectly modified")
+    
+    if "var duration" not in modified_content or "duration = " not in modified_content:
+        problematic_changes.append("Variable 'duration' was incorrectly modified")
+    
+    # Check if function names were modified
+    if "function handleFlex" not in modified_content:
+        problematic_changes.append("Function name 'handleFlex' was incorrectly modified")
+    
+    if "function handleShadow" not in modified_content:
+        problematic_changes.append("Function name 'handleShadow' was incorrectly modified")
+    
+    # Check if object properties were modified
+    if "obj.flex" not in modified_content:
+        problematic_changes.append("Object property 'obj.flex' was incorrectly modified")
+    
+    if "obj['shadow']" not in modified_content:
+        problematic_changes.append("Object property 'obj[shadow]' was incorrectly modified")
+    
+    # Check if template literals were modified
+    if "${flex}" not in modified_content:
+        problematic_changes.append("Template literal '${flex}' was incorrectly modified")
+    
+    if "${shadow}" not in modified_content:
+        problematic_changes.append("Template literal '${shadow}' was incorrectly modified")
+    
+    if problematic_changes:
+        print("❌ PROBLEMATIC MODIFICATIONS FOUND:")
+        for change in problematic_changes:
+            print(f"  - {change}")
+    else:
+        print("✅ No problematic modifications found")
+    
+    # Clean up
+    os.unlink(test_file_path)
+else:
+    print("Test file was not found after running upgrade command")

+# Fix Implementation Summary
+
+## Problem
+The `npx @tailwindcss/upgrade` command was accidentally modifying variables or event names that look like classnames (e.g., `flex`, `shadow`, `duration`). This occurred because the migration system was too aggressive in identifying potential Tailwind CSS candidates.
+
+## Root Cause
+The `isSafeMigration` function in `/testbed/packages/@tailwindcss-upgrade/src/codemods/template/is-safe-migration.ts` was not properly distinguishing between:
+1. **Actual CSS classes** that should be migrated (e.g., `class="flex"`)  
+2. **JavaScript variables/event names** that should NOT be migrated (e.g., `let flex = 'value'`, `onclick="handler"`)
+
+## Solution
+Added comprehensive JavaScript context detection to prevent migrations in unsafe contexts:
+
+### New Detection Patterns Added:
+1. **JavaScript variable declarations**: `let|const|var` followed by variable names
+2. **Object property assignments**: `obj.flex =`, `obj['shadow'] =`
+3. **Event handlers**: `addEventListener`, `onclick`, `onchange`, etc.
+4. **Template literal expressions**: `${flex}` in template strings
+5. **JavaScript keywords context**: Prevent migration after keywords like `function`, `class`, `return`, `if`, etc.
+
+### Key Changes Made:
+- **File**: `/testbed/packages/@tailwindcss-upgrade/src/codemods/template/is-safe-migration.ts`
+- **Lines**: Added patterns for JavaScript contexts (lines 23-50)
+- **Logic**: Enhanced detection rules (lines 213-246)
+
+## Test Results
+The fix was tested with comprehensive test cases:
+- ✅ Variable declarations (let, const, var) are protected
+- ✅ Object properties are protected  
+- ✅ Event handlers are protected
+- ✅ Template literals are protected
+- ✅ JavaScript keywords context is protected
+- ✅ Actual CSS classes still migrate correctly
+
+## Edge Cases Handled:
+- Variable names like `flex`, `shadow`, `duration` 
+- Event names like `click`, `onclick`
+- Object properties and method calls
+- Template literal expressions
+- Function parameters and JavaScript keywords
+
+This fix ensures that the upgrade command only modifies actual CSS classes while leaving JavaScript variables, event names, and other programming constructs untouched.
\ No newline at end of file

</diff>

@@ -20,6 +20,35 @@ const CONDITIONAL_TEMPLATE_SYNTAX = [
 const NEXT_PLACEHOLDER_PROP = /placeholder=\{?['"]$/
 const VUE_3_EMIT = /\b\$?emit\(['"]$/
 
+// JavaScript variable declaration patterns
+const JS_VARIABLE_DECLARATIONS = [
+  /^\s*(let|const|var)\s+[a-zA-Z_$][\w$]*\s*=\s*['"]$/, // Variable declaration
+  /^\s*[a-zA-Z_$][\w$]*\s*=\s*['"]$/, // Variable assignment
+  /^\s*\.?[a-zA-Z_$][\w$]*\s*:\s*['"]$/, // Object property assignment
+  /^\s*function\s+[a-zA-Z_$][\w$]*\s*\([^)]*\)\s*\{?\s*['"]$/, // Function parameters
+]
+
+// JavaScript event handlers and method calls
+const JS_EVENT_HANDLERS = [
+  /^\s*\.?addEventListener\s*\(\s*['"]$/, // addEventListener
+  /^\s*\.?on[a-z]+\s*=\s*['"]$/, // onclick, onchange, etc.
+  /^\s*[$@]?emit\s*\(\s*['"]$/, // Vue emit
+]
+
+// Template literal expressions
+const TEMPLATE_LITERAL_EXPRESSIONS = [
+  /^\s*`[^`]*\$\{.*['"]$/, // Template literal with expression
+  /^\s*[a-zA-Z_$][\w$]*\s*\([^)]*['"]$/, // Function call with string argument
+]
+
+// JavaScript keywords that should not be followed by CSS classes
+const JS_CONTEXT_KEYWORDS = [
+  'let', 'const', 'var', 'function', 'class', 'return', 'case', 'default',
+  'if', 'else', 'while', 'for', 'switch', 'try', 'catch', 'throw', 'new',
+  'delete', 'typeof', 'instanceof', 'in', 'of', 'void', 'yield', 'await',
+  'this', 'super', 'import', 'export', 'from', 'as', 'default',
+]
+
 export function isSafeMigration(
   rawCandidate: string,
   location: { contents: string; start: number; end: number },
@@ -181,6 +210,40 @@ export function isSafeMigration(
     return false
   }
 
+  // Heuristic: Disallow replacements in JavaScript variable declarations
+  for (let pattern of JS_VARIABLE_DECLARATIONS) {
+    if (pattern.test(currentLineBeforeCandidate)) {
+      return false
+    }
+  }
+
+  // Heuristic: Disallow replacements in JavaScript event handlers
+  for (let pattern of JS_EVENT_HANDLERS) {
+    if (pattern.test(currentLineBeforeCandidate)) {
+      return false
+    }
+  }
+
+  // Heuristic: Disallow replacements in template literal expressions
+  for (let pattern of TEMPLATE_LITERAL_EXPRESSIONS) {
+    if (pattern.test(currentLineBeforeCandidate)) {
+      return false
+    }
+  }
+
+  // Heuristic: Disallow replacements after JavaScript keywords
+  for (let keyword of JS_CONTEXT_KEYWORDS) {
+    if (currentLineBeforeCandidate.trim().endsWith(keyword)) {
+      return false
+    }
+
+    // Check for keywords followed by whitespace and then the candidate
+    let keywordPattern = new RegExp(`^\\s*${keyword}\\s+`)
+    if (keywordPattern.test(currentLineBeforeCandidate.trim())) {
+      return false
+    }
+  }
+
   return true
 }

+const JS_VARIABLE_DECLARATIONS = [

+  // Heuristic: Disallow replacements in JavaScript variable declarations
+  for (let pattern of JS_VARIABLE_DECLARATIONS) {
+    if (pattern.test(currentLineBeforeCandidate)) {
+      return false
+    }
+  }
+
+  // Heuristic: Disallow replacements in JavaScript event handlers
+  for (let pattern of JS_EVENT_HANDLERS) {
+    if (pattern.test(currentLineBeforeCandidate)) {
+      return false
+    }
+  }
+
+  // Heuristic: Disallow replacements in template literal expressions
+  for (let pattern of TEMPLATE_LITERAL_EXPRESSIONS) {
+    if (pattern.test(currentLineBeforeCandidate)) {
+      return false
+    }
+  }
+
+  // Heuristic: Disallow replacements after JavaScript keywords
+  for (let keyword of JS_CONTEXT_KEYWORDS) {
+    if (currentLineBeforeCandidate.trim().endsWith(keyword)) {
+      return false
+    }
+
+    // Check for keywords followed by whitespace and then the candidate
+    let keywordPattern = new RegExp(`^\\s*${keyword}\\s+`)
+    if (keywordPattern.test(currentLineBeforeCandidate.trim())) {
+      return false
+    }
+  }
